msg:This stay was a bad experience. The purpose of this hot spring trip was to take my parents and children to have a good rest and relax, but we were injured in the hand by the hair dryer in the hotel. The elderly and children were frightened all night and only slept for four or five hours, and were exhausted physically and mentally. Let me give an objective evaluation. In terms of hygiene: we booked a lake view room, and the balconies of both rooms were covered with dead mosquitoes. No one cleaned the room before check-in, so people with trypophobia should be careful. In terms of equipment: the hair dryer in the public area exploded, and it was in the hot spring area. There was no professional maintenance staff to check it. It was very scary to be in such a humid place where electric shock is very easy to happen. There were also problems such as the door locks and chandeliers in the guest rooms. It is hard to imagine that in a room that costs eight or nine hundred yuan a night, the balcony lock is difficult to open and the bedside chandelier is broken. In terms of service attitude: the hotel's housekeeping depar**ent, catering depar**ent and other service staff are still very heartwarming, but the attitude of the hotel leaders in dealing with problems is very chilling, and they tested our bottom line again and again. I think if the Cultural Tourism Bureau and the police station had not intervened, according to the negotiation plan given by the hotel at the beginning, they would only pay our medical expenses, and even the room fee would not be waived for us. If the subsequent itinerary had not been arranged, I think I would have stayed and had a good fight with them.

name:lâ€iâ€uâ€yâ€aâ€qâ€iâ€aâ€nâ€jâ€iâ€aâ€yâ€oâ€u
info:Garden-view Standard Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted February 13, 2024
msg:I started coming to this hot spring in 2014 and have been here many times. The hot springs are excellent, and the main feature is outdoor hot springs. There are more than 20 pools of different types outdoors, surrounded by dwarf pine and bamboo forests and other cold-resistant plants. The pools and layout are also antique, and because the location is far away from the city, there are no abrupt high-rise buildings around, and it is also very quiet, especially at night when you soak outdoors, the bamboo forest is swaying, the night sky is starry, and the outdoor hot spring experience should be the only one in Shandong Province; the disadvantage is that there are relatively few indoor pools, only one large and two small + a swimming pool. The disadvantage of the guest room is that the sound insulation is not good, especially the sound insulation of the room door is relatively poor, and any sound in the corridor can be heard.

The only drawback is that the breakfast is far worse than before. We were the first batch of guests when Tianmu Hot Spring just opened, and witnessed the growth of Tianmu Hot Spring. Tiantian is very cost-effective. The room price includes the hot spring ticket, which is worth the money.

msg:The room was OK. The parent-child room we stayed in had a tent and wooden horse specially prepared for children. It was very cozy, but the carpet and wooden horse were a bit dirty, so I didn't dare to let the children play.
We went there for the heavy snow and hot springs. When we went there, it happened to stop snowing. The thick snow was so beautiful. The children were so happy that they rolled around, dug holes, and stepped on footprints.
The hot springs are also great, especially the outdoor open-air hot springs. The stones and trees beside the pool are covered with thick snow. You can soak in the hot springs while looking at the snow scenery. The staff will also bring you hot ginger tea, which is perfect. .
The next morning, the child was very happy to join the work of shoveling snow in the hotel. He worked so enthusiastically that he couldn't help but persuade him, haha.
We will come again next year if it snows heavily.
